                        INNER JOIN "Avs_Circuit" C ON C."Super1"=
                        ) B
                        INNER JOIN F100 A ON A.F10003=B.F10003
                        LEFT JOIN F002 C ON A.F10002 = C.F00202

                        LEFT JOIN F004 G ON A.F10005 = G.F00405

                        LEFT JOIN F006 I ON A.F10007 = I.F00607

Eroarea:   MERGE INTO "Ptj_intrari" USING 
                            (select case when (SELECT count(*) FROM "Ptj_Intrari" WHERE f10003 = 6845 and "Ziua" = caldate) = 0 then 0 else 1 end as prezenta, 
                            a.*, b.* from  Z_Calendar a
                            left join 

                            (SELECT P."Zi", P."ZiSapt", CASE WHEN D.DAY IS NOT NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS "ZiLiberaLegala",
                            CASE WHEN P."ZiSapt"=6 OR P."ZiSapt"=7 OR D.DAY IS NOT NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS "ZiLibera", 
                            CASE WHEN COALESCE(b.ZL,0) <> 0 AND P."ZiSapt" < 6 AND (CASE WHEN D.DAY IS NOT NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) = 0 THEN 1 ELSE 
                            CASE WHEN COALESCE(b.S,0) <> 0 AND P."ZiSapt" = 6 THEN 1 ELSE 
                            CASE WHEN COALESCE(b.D,0) <> 0 AND P."ZiSapt" = 7 THEN 1 ELSE
                            CASE WHEN COALESCE(b.SL,0) <> 0 AND (CASE WHEN D.DAY IS NOT NULL THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) = 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 
                            END
                            END
                            END
                            END AS "AreDrepturi", "DenumireScurta"
                            FROM "tblZile" P
                            INNER JOIN "Ptj_tblAbsente" A ON 1=1
                            INNER JOIN "Ptj_ContracteAbsente" B ON A."Id" = B."IdAbsenta"
                            LEFT JOIN HOLIDAYS D on P."Zi"=D.DAY
                            WHERE CONVERT(date,'2022-12-01') <= CAST(P."Zi" AS date) AND CAST(P."Zi" AS date) <= CONVERT(date,'2022-12-31')
                            AND A."Id" = 4
                            AND COALESCE(A."DenumireScurta", '~') <> '~'
                            AND B."IdContract" = (SELECT MAX("IdContract") FROM "F100Contracte" WHERE F10003 =  6845 AND "DataInceput" <= CONVERT(date,'2022-12-01') AND CONVERT(date,'2022-12-31') <= "DataSfarsit") 
                            ) b
                            on a.caldate = b."Zi"

                            where caldate between  CONVERT(date,'2022-12-01') AND    CONVERT(date,'2022-12-31') and "AreDrepturi" = 1

                            ) Tmp 
                            ON ("Ptj_Intrari"."Ziua" = Tmp.caldate and prezenta = 1) 
                            WHEN MATCHED THEN UPDATE SET "ValStr" = "DenumireScurta"
                            WHEN NOT MATCHED THEN INSERT (F10003, "Ziua", "ZiSapt", "ZiLibera", "ZiLiberaLegala", "IdContract", "Norma", F10002, F10004, F10005, F10006, F10007, F06204, "ValStr", USER_NO, TIME)
                             VALUES (6845, tmp.caldate, "ZiSapt" ,"ZiLibera" , "ZiLiberaLegala", 
                            (SELECT X."IdContract" FROM "F100Contracte" X WHERE X.F10003 = 6845 AND X."DataInceput" <= tmp.caldate AND tmp.caldate <= X."DataSfarsit"), 
                            (SELECT F10043 FROM F100 WHERE F10003 = 6845), 
                             (SELECT F10002 FROM F100 WHERE F10003 = 6845), 
                             (SELECT F10004 FROM F100 WHERE F10003 = 6845), 
                             (SELECT F10005 FROM F100 WHERE F10003 = 6845), 
                             (SELECT F10006 FROM F100 WHERE F10003 = 6845), 
                             (SELECT F10007 FROM F100 WHERE F10003 = 6845), 
                             -1,  "DenumireScurta", 3, GetDate())

- isnull(F4,0)
- isnull(F6,0)

  where an=ent.An and Luna=ent.Luna and ptj_cumulat.F10003 = ent.F10003)

join f100 on ptj_intrari.f10003 = f100.f10003 and cast(ziua as date) between f10022 and f10023

- isnull(F4,0)
- isnull(F6,0)
 from  ptj_cumulat inner join F100 on ptj_cumulat.F10003 = F100.F10003 
  where an=ent.An and Luna=ent.Luna and ptj_cumulat.F10003 = ent.F10003) 
                            FROM "Ptj_Cumulat" ent
                            WHERE  1=1  AND ent.F10003=6 AND ent."An"=2020 AND ent."Luna"=4;

 where year(Ziua)=ent.An AND MONTH(Ziua)=ent.Luna AND Ptj_intrari.F10003=ent.F10003) 
                            FROM "Ptj_Cumulat" ent
                            WHERE  1=1  AND ent.F10003=6 AND ent."An"=2020 AND ent."Luna"=4;

 from  ptj_cumulat 
  where an=ent.An and Luna=ent.Luna and ptj_cumulat.F10003 = ent.F10003)

where an=ent.An and Luna=ent.Luna and ptj_cumulat.F10003 = ent.F10003)

where an=ent.An and Luna=ent.Luna and ptj_cumulat.F10003 = ent.F10003)

UPDATE ent 
                            SET ent.F23 = ( SELECT Ramase FROM SituatieZileAbsente WHERE F10003=ent.F10003 AND An=YEAR(ent.DataInceput)) 
                            FROM "Ptj_Cumulat" ent
                            WHERE  1=1  AND ent.F10003=6 AND ent."An"=2020 AND ent."Luna"=4;
UPDATE ent 
                            SET ent.F43 = (select   f30 - cast (case when isnull(F100.F10043,0)=0 then  isnull(F15,0)/8  else   isnull(F11,0) /F100.F10043 end as int) - isnull(F1,0) - isnull(F2,0) - isnull(F3,0)
- isnull(F4,0)
- isnull(F6,0)
 from  ptj_cumulat inner join F100 on ptj_cumulat.F10003 = F100.F10003 
  where an=ent.An and Luna=ent.Luna and ptj_cumulat.F10003 = ent.F10003) 
                            FROM "Ptj_Cumulat" ent
                            WHERE  1=1  AND ent.F10003=6 AND ent."An"=2020 AND ent."Luna"=4;
UPDATE ent 
                            SET ent.F30 = (select sum (case when  zilibera >0 or  ZiLiberaLegala > 0  then 0 else 1 end) from ptj_intrari
join f100 on ptj_intrari.f10003 = f100.f10003 and cast(ziua as date) between f10022 and f10023
 where year(Ziua)=ent.An AND MONTH(Ziua)=ent.Luna AND Ptj_intrari.F10003=ent.F10003) 
                            FROM "Ptj_Cumulat" ent
                            WHERE  1=1  AND ent.F10003=6 AND ent."An"=2020 AND ent."Luna"=4;

                            SET ent.F5 = (SELECT SUM(CASE WHEN COALESCE(ValStr,'') = 'R' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END)    FROM Ptj_Intrari   WHERE year(Ziua)=ent.An AND MONTH(Ziua)=ent.Luna AND F10003=ent.F10003) 
                            FROM "Ptj_Cumulat" ent
                            WHERE  1=1  AND ent.F10003=6 AND ent."An"=2020 AND ent."Luna"=4;
UPDATE ent

UPDATE ent

 from  ptj_cumulat 
  where an=ent.An and Luna=ent.Luna and ptj_cumulat.F10003 = ent.F10003) 
                            FROM "Ptj_Cumulat" ent
                            WHERE  1=1  AND ent.F10003=6 AND ent."An"=2020 AND ent."Luna"=4;
UPDATE ent 
                            SET ent.F16 = (select isnull(F5,0) * isnull(F100.f100973,0) from Ptj_Cumulat inner join f100 on ptj_cumulat.F10003 = F100.F10003   where an=ent.An and Luna=ent.Luna and ptj_cumulat.F10003 = ent.F10003) 
                            FROM "Ptj_Cumulat" ent

UPDATE ent 
                            SET ent.F17 = (
select isnull(F12,0)*2 + isnull(F11,0) from Ptj_Cumulat 
where an=ent.An and Luna=ent.Luna and ptj_cumulat.F10003 = ent.F10003) 
                            FROM "Ptj_Cumulat" ent
                            WHERE  1=1  AND ent.F10003=6 AND ent."An"=2020 AND ent."Luna"=4;
UPDATE ent 
                            SET ent.F15 = (select (isnull(F30,0) - isnull(F14,0))* isnull(F100.f100973,0) from Ptj_Cumulat inner join f100 on ptj_cumulat.F10003 = F100.F10003 
where an=ent.An and Luna=ent.Luna and ptj_cumulat.F10003 = ent.F10003) 
                            FROM "Ptj_Cumulat" ent
                            WHERE  1=1  AND ent.F10003=6 AND ent."An"=2020 AND ent."Luna"=4;
UPDATE ent 
                            SET ent.F18 = (select (case when 2*isnull(f12,0)-isnull(f5,0)>0 then 2*isnull(f12,0)-isnull(f5,0) else 0 end)*F100.F100973 from Ptj_Cumulat inner join f100 on ptj_cumulat.F10003 = F100.F10003  
where an=ent.An and Luna=ent.Luna and ptj_cumulat.F10003 = ent.F10003) 
                            FROM "Ptj_Cumulat" ent
                            WHERE  1=1  AND ent.F10003=6 AND ent."An"=2020 AND ent."Luna"=4;
UPDATE ent 
                            SET ent.F19 = (select isnull(F5,0) - ((isnull(F12,0)*2) - isnull(F18,0)/F100.F100973) from Ptj_Cumulat inner join f100 on ptj_cumulat.F10003 = F100.F10003 
where an=ent.An and Luna=ent.Luna and ptj_cumulat.F10003 = ent.F10003) 
                            FROM "Ptj_Cumulat" ent
                            WHERE  1=1  AND ent.F10003=6 AND ent."An"=2020 AND ent."Luna"=4;
UPDATE ent 
                            SET ent.F20 = (select (case when isnull(f11,0)-isnull(f19,0)>0 then isnull(f11,0)-isnull(f19,0) else 0 end)*F100.F100973 
from Ptj_Cumulat inner join f100 on ptj_cumulat.F10003 = F100.F10003  
where an=ent.An and Luna=ent.Luna and ptj_cumulat.F10003 = ent.F10003) 
                            FROM "Ptj_Cumulat" ent
                            WHERE  1=1  AND ent.F10003=6 AND ent."An"=2020 AND ent."Luna"=4;
UPDATE ent 
                            SET ent.F21 = (Select isnull(F10,0)+isnull(F20,0) from Ptj_Cumulat where an=ent.An and Luna=ent.Luna and ptj_cumulat.F10003 = ent.F10003) 
                            FROM "Ptj_Cumulat" ent
                            WHERE  1=1  AND ent.F10003=6 AND ent."An"=2020 AND ent."Luna"=4;
UPDATE ent 
                            SET ent.F22 = (Select (isnull(F5,0)-isnull(F19,0))/2 from Ptj_Cumulat 
where an=ent.An and Luna=ent.Luna and ptj_cumulat.F10003 = ent.F10003) 
                            FROM "Ptj_Cumulat" ent
                            WHERE  1=1  AND ent.F10003=6 AND ent."An"=2020 AND ent."Luna"=4;
UPDATE ent 
                            SET ent.F23 = ( SELECT Ramase FROM SituatieZileAbsente WHERE F10003=ent.F10003 AND An=YEAR(ent.DataInceput)) 
                            FROM "Ptj_Cumulat" ent
                            WHERE  1=1  AND ent.F10003=6 AND ent."An"=2020 AND ent."Luna"=4;
UPDATE ent 
                            SET ent.F43 = (select   f30 - cast (case when isnull(F100.F10043,0)=0 then  isnull(F15,0)/8  else   isnull(F11,0) /F100.F10043 end as int) - isnull(F1,0) - isnull(F2,0) - isnull(F3,0)
- isnull(F4,0)
- isnull(F6,0)
 from  ptj_cumulat inner join F100 on ptj_cumulat.F10003 = F100.F10003 
  where an=ent.An and Luna=ent.Luna and ptj_cumulat.F10003 = ent.F10003) 
                            FROM "Ptj_Cumulat" ent
                            WHERE  1=1  AND ent.F10003=6 AND ent."An"=2020 AND ent."Luna"=4;
UPDATE ent 
                            SET ent.F30 = (select sum (case when  zilibera >0 or  ZiLiberaLegala > 0  then 0 else 1 end) from ptj_intrari
join f100 on ptj_intrari.f10003 = f100.f10003 and cast(ziua as date) between f10022 and f10023
 where year(Ziua)=ent.An AND MONTH(Ziua)=ent.Luna AND Ptj_intrari.F10003=ent.F10003) 
                            FROM "Ptj_Cumulat" ent
                            WHERE  1=1  AND ent.F10003=6 AND ent."An"=2020 AND ent."Luna"=4;

END;
